### [1] [The Depth Poset under Transpositions in the Filter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21961)
*Herbert Edelsbrunner,Michał Lipiński,Marian Mrozek,Manuel Soriano-Trigueros,Fedor Zimin*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文研究过滤Lefschetz复形深度偏序集的计算算法及其在细胞转置下的变化，结合Vineyard持久性理论分析随机点数据统计特性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究过滤Lefschetz复形中深度偏序集的计算效率及其在细胞转置下的稳定性，为拓扑数据分析提供更高效的算法工具

Method: 结合快速计算深度偏序集的算法和基于Vineyard持久性的转置更新方法，对细胞转置如何影响深度偏序集进行完整案例分析

Result: 提出了深度偏序集的高效计算算法，分析了细胞转置对深度偏序集的完整影响模式，并给出了随机点数据深度偏序集的统计特性及其在随机直线同伦下的敏感性

Conclusion: 深度偏序集的计算算法与Vineyard持久性理论相结合，为理解过滤复形中细胞转置对拓扑结构的影响提供了完整的理论框架和实用工具

Abstract: The depth poset of a filtered Lefschetz complex reflects the dependencies between the cancellations of different shallow birth-death pairs. Using the fast algorithms for computing the depth poset in the present work and for updating the persistence diagram under transpositions (Vineyard persistence), we give a complete case analysis of how transpositions of cells in the filter affect the depth poset. In addition, we present statistics on the depth poset for random point data and its sensitivity to the transpositions that occur in random straight-line homotopies.

</details>


### [2] [Posets of decompositions in spherical buildings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22531)
*Kevin Ivan Piterman,John Shareshian,Volkmar Welker*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 论文将向量空间的分解偏序集和公共基复形概念推广到任意球面建筑，证明了分解偏序集的Cohen-Macaulay性质以及部分分解偏序集的球面性和同伦等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将线性情况（向量空间）中已知的分解偏序集和公共基复形构造推广到任意球面建筑，扩展这些组合几何结构在更一般建筑理论中的应用。

Method: 基于球面建筑理论，利用对立性、Levi球面和凸性等概念，定义了任意球面建筑的公共基复形、分解偏序集和部分分解偏序集，并分析它们的组合拓扑性质。

Result: 证明了分解偏序集是Cohen-Macaulay的，部分分解偏序集是球面的且与公共基复形同伦等价，同时发现有序部分分解偏序集承载Steinberg表示的平方。

Conclusion: 成功将线性情况的构造推广到任意球面建筑，建立了这些组合几何对象的一般理论框架，揭示了它们与建筑理论中对立性、凸性等概念的深刻联系。

Abstract: We propose definitions of the common bases complex, the poset of decompositions, and the poset of partial decompositions for arbitrary spherical buildings. We show that the poset of decompositions is Cohen-Macaulay, and that the poset of partial decompositions is spherical and homotopy equivalent to the common bases complex. To prove these results, we rely on the concepts of opposition, Levi spheres, and convexity in buildings.
  In particular, our results extend the already known constructions for the linear case (vector spaces) to arbitrary buildings. As a byproduct, we see that the poset of ordered partial decompositions carries the square of the Steinberg representation.

</details>


### [3] [On the Classification of $S^3$-Bundles over $\mathbb{C}P^2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22999)
*Wancheng Liu*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 该论文对S^3-丛在CP^2上的全空间进行了定向保持同伦等价分类


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究S^3-丛在复射影平面CP^2上的全空间的同伦等价分类问题，这是微分拓扑和几何拓扑中的重要课题

Method: 采用两步法：首先通过计算Kreck-Stolz不变量得到PL同胚分类，然后基于PL分类结果应用手术理论建立同伦等价分类

Result: 成功完成了S^3-丛在CP^2上全空间的定向保持同伦等价分类

Conclusion: 通过结合PL分类和手术理论，系统解决了这类流形的同伦等价分类问题，为相关拓扑研究提供了重要工具

Abstract: This paper presents a classification of the total spaces of $S^3$-bundles over $\mathbb{C}P^2$ up to orientation-preserving homotopy equivalence. Our approach proceeds in two steps: we first derive the PL-homeomorphism classification for these manifolds by computing their Kreck-Stolz invariants. Then, building upon this PL classification result and through an application of surgery theory, we establish the homotopy equivalence classification.

</details>

### [4] [Concentrated real-pole uniform-in-time approximation of the matrix exponential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21858)
*Stefan Güttel,Shuai Shao*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种渐近最优的共享集中实极点选择方法，用于有理逼近时间相关指数函数exp(-tz)，扩展了Andersson关于exp(-z)有理逼近的经典结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究时间相关指数函数exp(-tz)的有理逼近问题，寻求在正时间区间T内对z≥0的渐近最优逼近方法，扩展Andersson关于exp(-z)有理逼近的经典理论。

Method: 提出一种渐近最优的共享集中实极点选择策略，用于构造时间相关指数函数的有理逼近族。通过数值实验验证该方法在不同时间范围和逼近阶数下的性能。

Result: 数值实验表明，所提出的集中实极点选择方法在各种时间范围和不同逼近阶数下都表现出接近最优的性能。该方法还可应用于线性常系数初值问题的均匀时间有理逼近。

Conclusion: 成功扩展了Andersson的经典结果，为时间相关指数函数的有理逼近提供了一种渐近最优的实极点选择方法，在理论和应用上都具有重要意义。

Abstract: We propose an asympotically optimal choice of shared concentrated real poles of a family of rational approximants of time-dependent exponential functions $\exp(-tz)$ for $z \geq 0$ and $t$ in a positive time interval $T$. Our result extends a classical result by J.-E.Andersson [J.Approx.Theory, 32(2):85--95, 1981] on the asymptotic best rational approximation of $\exp(-z)$ with real poles. Numerical experiments demonstrate the near-optimality of our choice for various time ranges and for both small and large approximation degrees. An application of the uniform-in-time rational approximation using our proposed concentrated real poles to a linear constant-coefficient initial-value problem is also discussed.

</details>


### [5] [BDF2-type integrator for Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation in micromagnetics, part I: unconditional weak convergence to weak solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22000)
*Michele Aldé,Michael Feischl,Dirk Praetorius*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了一种求解Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程的全离散方法，结合空间一阶有限元和时间BDF2两步法，每时间步只需解一个线性系统，证明了无条件稳定性并收敛到弱解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert方程是描述微磁现象的重要模型，需要开发高效稳定的数值方法。现有方法可能计算复杂或稳定性不足，需要设计每时间步只需解一个线性系统的高效算法。

Method: 采用空间一阶有限元离散和时间BDF2两步法，通过时间线性插值重构离散时空磁化强度。每时间步只需解一个线性系统，算法实现简单高效。

Result: 证明了积分器的无条件稳定性，重构磁化强度的子序列在时空域中弱收敛于LLG的弱解。数值实验验证了空间一阶精度和时间二阶精度。

Conclusion: 提出了一种高效稳定的LLG方程全离散数值方法，具有无条件稳定性和收敛性，计算效率高，数值精度满足预期。

Abstract: We consider the Landau-Lifshitz-Gilbert equation (LLG) that models time-dependent micromagnetic phenomena. We propose a full discretization that employs first-order finite elements in space and a BDF2-type two-step method in time. In each time step, only one linear system of equations has to be solved. We employ linear interpolation in time to reconstruct the discrete space-time magnetization. We prove that the integrator is unconditionally stable and thus guarantees that a subsequence of the reconstructed magnetization converges weakly in $H^1$ towards a weak solution of LLG in the space-time domain. Numerical experiments verify that the proposed integrator is indeed first-order in space and second-order in time.

</details>


### [6] [Broken-FEEC on multipatch domains with local refinements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22206)
*Martin Campos Pinto,Frederik Schnack*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于局部细化样条空间和非匹配界面的broken-FEEC新方法，通过保持矩的离散保形投影算子消除数值伪影，实现能量守恒的麦克斯韦求解器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统broken-FEEC允许在单元界面处不连续离散化，保持de Rham结构并提供计算优势，但局部细化常导致数值伪影，需要解决非匹配界面的连续性问题。

Method: 开发了保持矩的离散保形投影算子，这些算子具有显式、局部化和度量无关的特性，确保在非匹配界面上保持H¹和H(curl)连续性，同时保持高阶多项式矩。

Result: 获得了具有精确强导数和弱导数的broken-FEEC de Rham序列，实现了显式的能量守恒麦克斯韦求解器，几乎消除了伪模式。数值模拟证实了该方法能有效消除伪波。

Conclusion: 该方法成功扩展了broken-FEEC到局部细化样条空间，通过保持矩的投影算子解决了非匹配界面的连续性问题，为电磁场计算提供了高效无伪影的数值方法。

Abstract: This article introduces a novel approach for broken-FEEC (Finite Element Exterior Calculus), extending its application to locally refined spline spaces with non-matching interfaces. Traditional broken-FEEC allows for discontinuous discretizations at patch interfaces, preserving the de Rham structure and offering computational benefits. However, local refinements often lead to numerical artifacts. Our solution involves developing moment-preserving discrete conforming projection operators. These operators are explicit, localized, and metric-independent, ensuring $H^1$ and $H(\text{curl})$ continuity across non-matching interfaces while preserving high-order polynomial moments. This results in broken-FEEC de Rham sequences with accurate strong and weak derivatives, leading to energy-preserving Maxwell solvers that are explicit and virtually free of spurious modes. Numerical simulations confirm the efficacy of our method in eliminating spurious waves.

</details>


### [7] [The Reduced Basis Multigrid scheme for the Virtual Element Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22219)
*Paola F. Antonietti,Silvia Bertoluzza,Fabio Credali*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于多边形网格上最低阶虚拟单元方法的非嵌套W循环多重网格方案，通过简化基方法计算虚拟基函数构建完全共形辅助空间，避免虚拟单元空间的隐式定义问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虚拟单元方法在多边形网格上具有优势，但其虚拟单元空间的隐式定义给多重网格方法中的网格间算子计算带来困难，需要解决这一问题以提高计算效率。

Method: 使用简化基方法廉价计算虚拟基函数，构建完全共形的辅助空间，在此基础上设计非嵌套W循环多重网格方案，避免直接处理虚拟单元空间的隐式定义问题。

Result: 成功实现了多边形网格上最低阶虚拟单元方法的多重网格方案，通过辅助空间方法有效解决了网格间算子计算的难题。

Conclusion: 提出的非嵌套W循环多重网格方案为虚拟单元方法提供了有效的求解器，通过简化基方法构建辅助空间的方法为解决虚拟单元空间隐式定义问题提供了新思路。

Abstract: We present a non-nested W-cycle multigrid scheme for the lowest order Virtual Element Method on polygonal meshes. To avoid the implicit definition of the Virtual Element space, which poses several issues in the computation of intergrid operators that underpin multigrid methods, the proposed scheme uses a fully-conforming auxiliary space constructed by cheaply computing the virtual basis functions via the reduced basis method.

</details>


### [8] [High-Order Asymptotic-Preserving IMEX schemes for an ES-BGK model for Gas Mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22304)
*Domenico Caparello,Lorenzo Pareschi,Thomas Rey*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文构建了用于气体混合物ES-BGK模型的高阶渐近保持(AP)隐式-显式(IMEX)格式，该格式在任意克努森数下保持稳定，在流体极限下退化为混合物宏观方程的高阶精确求解器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对气体混合物ES-BGK模型，需要开发一种能够处理从稀薄到连续流全流区的高阶数值方法，克服松弛项带来的刚度问题，同时保持渐近保持特性。

Method: 基于Filbet和Jin的单组分BGK模型IMEX策略，扩展到多组分ES-BGK设置；采用三阶时间积分、CWENO3有限体积空间重构、离散速度空间中宏观矩的精确守恒，以及多线程实现。

Result: 方法完全显式、在任意克努森数下均匀稳定，时间步长仅受双曲CFL条件约束；能够处理任意数量的组分，在多维气体混合物动力学测试中验证了AP特性和正确的渐近行为。

Conclusion: 成功构建了适用于气体混合物ES-BGK模型的高阶AP IMEX格式，该方法在稀薄和连续流区均表现出良好的精度和鲁棒性，为多组分气体动力学模拟提供了有效工具。

Abstract: In this work we construct a high-order Asymptotic-Preserving (AP) Implicit-Explicit (IMEX) scheme for the ES-BGK model for gas mixtures introduced in [Brull, Commun. Math. Sci., 2015]. The time discretization is based on the IMEX strategy proposed in [Filbet, Jin, J. Sci. Comput., 2011] for the single-species BGK model and is here extended to the multi-species ES-BGK setting. The resulting method is fully explicit, uniformly stable with respect to the Knudsen number and, in the fluid regime, it reduces to a consistent and high-order accurate solver for the limiting macroscopic equations of the mixture. The IMEX structure removes the stiffness associated with the relaxation term so that the time step is constrained only by a hyperbolic CFL condition. The full solver couples a high-order space and velocity discretization that includes third-order time integration, a CWENO3 finite-volume reconstruction in space, exact conservation of macroscopic moments in the discrete velocity space, and a multithreaded implementation. The proposed approach can handle an arbitrary number of species. Its accuracy and robustness are demonstrated on a set of multidimensional kinetic tests for gas mixtures, where the AP property and the correct asymptotics are numerically verified across different regimes.

</details>


### [9] [Weyl distributions, spectral properties, and circulant approximation results for quaternion block multilevel Toeplitz matrix sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22422)
*Ayoub Lailoune,Valerio Loi,Stefano Serra-Capizzano*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该论文全面研究了由s×t四元数矩阵值、d变量、Lebesgue可积生成函数生成的单轴四元数块多层Toeplitz矩阵序列的Weyl特征值和奇异值分布，并提出了四元数矩阵序列的近似类序列概念，为大规模四元数线性系统的快速预处理方法奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代应用中产生的大规模四元数线性系统需要有效的预处理方法。四元数块多层Toeplitz矩阵序列在信号处理、图像处理等领域有广泛应用，但缺乏系统的特征值分布理论和有效的近似预处理技术。

Method: 1. 将近似类序列概念扩展到四元数矩阵序列，允许将矩阵与其预处理器之间的差异分解为低范数加相对低秩项；2. 将四元数块多层循环矩阵序列作为四元数块多层Toeplitz矩阵序列的近似类序列；3. 建立Weyl特征值和奇异值分布理论；4. 通过数值实验验证方法有效性。

Result: 1. 建立了四元数矩阵序列的近似类序列理论框架；2. 证明了四元数块多层循环矩阵序列可作为四元数块多层Toeplitz矩阵序列的有效近似；3. 为大规模四元数线性系统提供了快速预处理方法的理论基础；4. 数值实验验证了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究为四元数块多层Toeplitz矩阵序列提供了完整的Weyl特征值和奇异值分布理论，并通过扩展近似类序列概念建立了有效的矩阵近似和预处理框架，为处理现代应用中产生的大规模四元数线性系统提供了理论基础和实用方法，并指出了未来研究方向。

Abstract: The present work contains a comprehensive treatment of Weyl eigenvalue and singular value distributions for single-axis quaternion block multilevel Toeplitz matrix sequences generated by $s\times t$ quaternion matrix-valued, $d$-variate, Lebesgue integrable generating functions. Furthermore, in view of concrete applications, we are interested in preconditioning and matrix approximation results. To this end, a crucial step is the extension of the notion of an approximating class of sequences (a.c.s.) to the case of matrix sequences with quaternion entries, since it allows us to decompose the difference between a matrix and its preconditioner into low-norm plus (relatively) low-rank terms. As a specific example, we consider classes of quaternion block multilevel circulant matrix sequences as an a.c.s. for quaternion block multilevel Toeplitz matrix sequences. These approximation results lay the foundations for fast preconditioning methods when dealing with large quaternion linear systems stemming from modern applications. We conclude our study with numerical experiments and directions for future research.

</details>


### [10] [Parabolic hysteresis problems revisited: Finite element error analysis and convergent Newton-type solvers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22424)
*Shu Xu,Liqun Cao*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该论文首次对含迟滞的抛物型偏微分方程建立了有限元误差估计，并开发了高效的阻尼平滑牛顿求解器，实现了全局收敛和局部Q-二次收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往对含迟滞偏微分方程的数值研究主要集中在模拟方面，缺乏数值误差分析，且主要依赖无导数非线性求解器。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立严格的有限元误差估计并开发高效求解器。

Method: 采用向后欧拉全离散格式处理半线性和拟线性抛物方程中的连续迟滞算子。为处理非线性代数系统的固有非光滑性，开发了基于平滑逼近一般条件的阻尼平滑牛顿求解器。

Result: 建立了严格的有限元误差估计，数值实验证实了半线性问题的理论收敛率，而拟线性问题显示出高于预期的收敛阶。所提求解器在鲁棒性和效率方面优于现有方法。

Conclusion: 本文首次为含迟滞的抛物型偏微分方程提供了系统的数值分析框架，包括误差估计和高效求解算法，填补了该领域的理论空白，为实际应用提供了可靠的计算工具。

Abstract: Numerical investigations of partial differential equations with hysteresis have largely focused on simulations, leaving numerical error analysis unexplored and relying mainly on derivative-free nonlinear solvers. This work establishes rigorous finite element error estimates for the backward Euler fully discrete scheme applied to semilinear and quasilinear parabolic equations involving continuous hysteresis operators. To efficiently handle the inherent nonsmoothness of the resulting nonlinear algebraic systems, we develop a damped smoothing Newton solver under a general condition on the smoothing approximation, ensuring global convergence together with local Q-quadratic convergence. Numerical experiments confirm the theoretical convergence rates for semilinear problems, while showing higher-than-predicted orders for quasilinear ones. The robustness and efficiency of the proposed solver are further demonstrated in comparison with existing methods.

</details>


### [11] [Piecewise polynomial approximation on non-Lipschitz domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22628)
*D P Hewett*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在非Lipschitz域的非Lipschitz网格上，分片不连续多项式逼近在分数阶Sobolev空间中的最佳逼近误差估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统逼近理论通常假设域和网格具有Lipschitz边界，但在实际应用中常遇到非Lipschitz边界（如分形边界）的情况。需要建立更一般的逼近理论框架来处理这些复杂几何结构。

Method: 在非Lipschitz域上使用非Lipschitz网格，允许域边界和网格单元边界为分形结构。研究分片不连续多项式在分数阶Sobolev空间中的逼近性质。

Result: 证明了在非Lipschitz域的非Lipschitz网格上，分片不连续多项式逼近在分数阶Sobolev空间中的最佳逼近误差估计，扩展了经典逼近理论的应用范围。

Conclusion: 该研究为处理具有复杂几何结构（包括分形边界）的偏微分方程数值解提供了理论基础，扩展了有限元方法在非标准几何域上的适用性。

Abstract: We prove best approximation error estimates for discontinuous piecewise polynomial approximation in fractional Sobolev spaces on non-Lipschitz meshes of non-Lipschitz domains. In particular, the boundary of the domain, and the boundaries of the mesh elements, can be fractal.

</details>

Abstract: The paper considers function-valued tensors, viewed as multidimensional arrays with entries in an abstract Hilbert space. A key feature of our approach is the careful design of so-called quantities of interest, defining functionals of the solution whose values the multiscale approximation aims to reproduce exactly. Conclusion: 本文成功设计了一种五阶混合快速扫描AWENO方法，利用定点快速扫描的显式特性和不等长子模板的AWENO方案，结合非线性与线性格式的混合技术，显著提高了求解双曲守恒律稳态问题的收敛性和计算效率，为高精度稳态计算提供了有效工具。

Abstract: In this paper, we extend the previous work on absolutely convergent fixed-point fast sweeping WENO methods by Li et al. (J. Comput. Phys. 443: 110516, 2021) and design a fifth-order hybrid fast sweeping scheme for solving steady state problems of hyperbolic conservation laws. Unlike many other fast sweeping methods, the explicit property of fixed-point fast sweeping methods provides flexibility to apply the alternative weighted essentially non-oscillatory (AWENO) scheme with unequal-sized substencils as the local solver, which facilitates the usage of arbitrary monotone numerical fluxes. Furthermore, a novel hybrid technique is designed in the local solver to combine the nonlinear AWENO interpolation with the linear scheme for an additional improvement in efficiency of the high-order fast sweeping iterations. Numerical examples show that the developed fixed-point fast sweeping hybrid AWENO method with unequal-sized substencils can achieve absolute convergence (i.e., the residue of the fast sweeping iterations converges to machine zero / round off errors) more easily than the original AWENO method with equal-sized substencils, and is more efficient than the popular third-order total variation diminishing (TVD) Runge-Kutta time-marching approach to converge to steady state solutions.

### [15] [A structure-preserving semi-implicit four-split scheme for continuum mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23015)
*Michael Dumbser,Andrea Thomann,Maurizio Tavelli,Walter Boscheri*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的结构保持顶点交错半隐式四分裂离散化方法，用于统一的一阶双曲型连续介质力学公式，能够同时描述流体和固体材料，时间步长仅受材料速度限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的结构保持离散化方法虽然能保持无旋特性和低马赫数极限一致性，但热脉冲和畸变场的演化仍采用显式离散，导致时间步长受到剪切声速和热波速度的严格CFL限制。需要开发一种更高效的方法来放宽时间步长限制。

Method: 将控制PDE系统分裂为四个子系统：1) 对流子系统（显式处理）；2) 热子系统（隐式）；3) 包含动量、畸变场和特定热脉冲的子系统（隐式）；4) 压力子系统（隐式）。采用顶点交错半隐式四分裂离散化方法，仅对流部分需要显式处理。

Result: 新方法的时间步长限制仅基于连续介质的速度，相比之前基于剪切声速和热波速度的严格CFL限制大为放宽。方法在低马赫数极限和刚性松弛极限下保持渐近一致性，在线性源项或没有源项时保持精确无旋的畸变场和热脉冲。

Conclusion: 提出的四分裂半隐式方案显著改善了计算效率，通过将大部分子系统隐式处理，仅对流部分显式处理，实现了仅基于材料速度的时间步长限制，同时保持了理论特性和结构保持性质。

Abstract: We introduce a novel structure-preserving vertex-staggered semi-implicit four-split discretization of a unified first order hyperbolic formulation of continuum mechanics that is able to describe at the same time fluid and solid materials within the same mathematical model. The governing PDE system goes back to pioneering work of Godunov, Romenski, Peshkov and collaborators. Previous structure-preserving discretizations of this system allowed to respect the curl-free properties of the distortion field and the specific thermal impulse in the absence of source terms and were consistent with the low Mach number limit with respect to the adiabatic sound speed. However, the evolution of the thermal impulse and the distortion field were still discretized explicitly, thus requiring a rather severe CFL stability restriction on the time step based on the shear sound speed and the finite, but potentially large, speed of heat waves. Instead, the new four-split semi-implicit scheme presented in this paper has a material time step restriction only. For this purpose, the governing PDE system is split into four subsystems: i) a convective subsystem, which is the only one that is treated explicitly; ii) a heat subsystem, iii) a subsystem containing momentum, distortion field and specific thermal impulse; iv) a pressure subsystem. The three subsystems ii)-iv) are all discretized implicitly, hence a rather mild CFL restriction based on the velocity of the continuum is imposed. The method is asymptotically consistent with the low Mach number limit and the stiff relaxation limits. Moreover, it maintains an exactly curl-free distortion field and thermal impulse in the case of linear source terms or in their absence. The scheme is benchmarked against classical test cases verifying its theoretical properties.

</details>

*Julian Koellermeier,Michael Redle,Manuel Torrilhon*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将浅水矩方程扩展到任意阶磁旋转浅水系统，使用多项式展开表示速度和磁场的垂直剖面，通过Galerkin投影得到多项式系数的演化方程来闭合系统。

Abstract: Originally introduced to describe a transition region in stars, the magnetic rotating shallow water (MRSW) model is now used in many solar physics and geophysical applications. Derived from the 3-D incompressible magnetohydrodynamic system, the shallow nature of these applications motivates depth-averaging of both the velocities and magnetic fields. This is advantageous in terms of computational efficiency -- but at the loss of vertical information, thus limiting the predictive power of the MRSW model. To overcome this problem, we employ higher-order vertical moments, but now in the context of conductive fluids. In doing so, the new approximation maintains non-constant vertical profiles of both the horizontal magnetic fields and horizontal velocities, while still remaining in the simplified 2-D framework corresponding to depth integration. In this work, we extend the derivation of the shallow water moment equations to derive the MRSW moment system of arbitrary order; i.e., we represent the vertical profiles of the velocities -- and now additionally the magnetic fields -- by arbitrary-order polynomial expansions, and close the new expanded 2-D system with evolution equations for these polynomial coefficients, found via Galerkin projection. Through numerical experiments for MRSW moment systems up to third-order, we demonstrate that these moment approximations reduce model error without significantly sacrificing computational efficiency.

### [18] [Conservative and dissipative discretisations of multi-conservative ODEs and GENERIC systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23266)
*Boris D. Andrews,Patrick E. Farrell*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出两种方法：(1) 针对一般保守常微分方程的任意阶时间离散化，通过系统引入辅助变量，在离散层面复制守恒证明；(2) 针对GENERIC格式（包含泊松系统和梯度下降系统）的能量守恒和熵耗散格式，同样通过辅助变量实现离散层面的结构保持。

Abstract: Partial differential equations (PDEs) describing thermodynamically isolated systems typically possess conserved quantities (like mass, momentum, and energy) and dissipated quantities (like entropy). Preserving these conservation and dissipation laws on discretisation in time can yield vastly better approximations for the same computational effort, compared to schemes that are not structure-preserving. In this work we present two novel contributions: (i) an arbitrary-order time discretisation for general conservative ordinary differential equations that conserves all known invariants and (ii) an energy-conserving and entropy-dissipating scheme for both ordinary and partial differential equations written in the GENERIC format, a superset of Poisson and gradient-descent systems. In both cases the underlying strategy is the same: the systematic introduction of auxiliary variables, allowing for the replication at the discrete level of the proofs of conservation or dissipation. We illustrate the advantages of our approximations with numerical examples of the Kepler and Kovalevskaya problems, a combustion engine model, and the Benjamin-Bona-Mahony equation.

### [19] [LR B-spline perspective for RM B-splines: construction and effortless refinements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23412)
*Francesco Patrizi*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RM B-splines具有局部线性独立性和快速de Boor类评估算法，适用于等几何分析，但需要建立自动网格细化方法

Method: 通过观察RM B-splines是Locally Refined (LR) B-splines的特殊情况，建立自动网格细化程序

Result: 证明了RM B-splines是LR B-splines的子集，因此可以利用LR B-splines的现有网格细化技术

Conclusion: RM B-splines作为LR B-splines的特殊情况，可以轻松实现自动网格细化，增强了其在等几何分析中的应用价值

Abstract: Reachable Minimally supported (RM) B-splines have been recently introduced as a novel B-spline--like basis. They feature local linear independence and admit a fast de Boor--like evaluation algorithm. These properties make them particularly attractive for applications in isogeometric analysis. In this note, we show that automatic mesh refinement procedures can be readily established by observing that RM B-splines are a special case of Locally Refined (LR) B-splines.

### [20] [Thermodynamics of the Heisenberg antiferromagnet on the maple-leaf lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21806)
*Robin Schäfer,Paul L. Ebert,Noah Hassan,Johannes Reuther,David J. Luitz,Alexander Wietek*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文使用数值关联团簇展开（NLCE）等多种数值方法研究枫叶晶格上的海森堡反铁磁体，发现NLCE具有非常规的收敛性，可延伸至低温甚至零温。研究发现比热容在T1≈0.479J和T2≈0.131J处呈现双峰结构，自旋-自旋结构因子在中间温度下反映晶格缺乏反射对称性的特征。零温收敛表明基态为短程关联的顺磁态，由共振六边形图案组成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究枫叶晶格上海森堡反铁磁体的热力学性质和基态特性，探索非传统晶格结构对磁系统行为的影响，特别是缺乏反射对称性的晶格如何影响自旋关联和热力学响应。

Method: 采用多种数值方法：数值关联团簇展开（NLCE）、伪马约拉纳泛函重整化群、有限温度Lanczos方法和经典蒙特卡洛模拟。NLCE作为主要方法，具有非常规的低温收敛特性，用于计算热力学性质和自旋-自旋关联函数。

Result: 比热容在T1≈0.479J和T2≈0.131J处呈现双峰结构，类似于三角晶格的结果。中间温度下自旋-自旋结构因子显示晶格缺乏反射对称性的特征。NLCE的零温收敛提供了可靠的基态能量估计，表明基态为短程关联的顺磁态，由共振六边形图案组成。

Conclusion: 枫叶晶格上的海森堡反铁磁体具有独特的热力学行为，比热容双峰结构反映了系统的能级特征。自旋关联模式揭示了晶格对称性缺失的影响。基态为短程关联的顺磁态，由共振六边形图案构成，这一发现为理解非传统晶格上的量子磁性提供了新见解。

Abstract: We study the Heisenberg antiferromagnet on the maple-leaf lattice using several numerical approaches, focusing on the numerical linked-cluster expansion (NLCE), which exhibits an unconventional convergence extending to low and even zero temperatures. We evaluate thermodynamic properties as well as spin-spin correlations through the equal-time structure factor. Within NLCE the specific heat capacity reveals a two-peak structure at $T_1 \approx 0.479\,J$ and $T_2 \approx 0.131\,J$, reminiscent of the corresponding result for the triangular lattice. At intermediate temperatures, the spin-spin structure factor develops features that reflect the absence of reflection symmetry in the lattice. The zero-temperature convergence of NLCE enables reliable estimates of the ground-state energy and points to a short-range correlated paramagnetic ground state composed of resonating hexagonal motifs. The NLCE results are benchmarked against Pseudo-Majorana Functional Renormalization Group, finite-temperature Lanczos, and classical Monte Carlo simulations.

</details>


### [21] [Obstruction to Ergodicity from Locality and $U(1)$ Higher Symmetries on the Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21815)
*Ramanjit Sohal,Ruben Verresen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 在具有局域相互作用和有限格点希尔伯特空间维度的晶格系统中，任何精确的U(1)高阶对称性都会阻碍幺正动力学下的遍历性，导致希尔伯特空间碎片化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高阶对称性对量子系统遍历性的影响，解释在量子链接模型等系统中观察到的遍历性破缺现象。

Method: 基于对称性的方法，不依赖于哈密顿量和晶格的具体细节。专注于二维情况，明确构造Krylov子空间，并识别表征这些子空间的涌现守恒量。

Result: 证明了具有精确U(1)高阶对称性的系统必然表现出希尔伯特空间碎片化，其Krylov子空间数量随系统尺寸指数增长。这些子空间不能通过对称性量子数区分，但可以通过涌现的守恒量来表征。

Conclusion: 任何精确的U(1)高阶对称性都会对局域相互作用有限维晶格系统的遍历性产生根本性阻碍，这为一系列系统中的遍历性破缺提供了系统性解释。

Abstract: We argue that the presence of \emph{any} exact $U(1)$ higher-form symmetry, under mild assumptions, presents a fundamental obstruction to ergodicity under unitary dynamics in lattice systems with local interactions and finite on-site Hilbert space dimension. Focusing on the two-dimensional case, we show that such systems necessarily exhibit Hilbert space fragmentation and explicitly construct Krylov sectors whose number scales exponentially with system size. While these sectors cannot be distinguished by symmetry quantum numbers, we identify the emergent integrals of motion which characterize them. Our symmetry-based approach is insensitive to details of the Hamiltonian and the lattice, providing a systematic explanation for ergodicity-breaking in a range of systems, including quantum link models.

Method: 使用光谱成像扫描隧道显微镜，通过在不同晶格位点引入化学取代来抑制电荷密度波相，研究CsV₃Sb₅在不同掺杂浓度下的相图。

Result: 在所有样品中，即使电荷密度波被完全抑制后，电子结构的旋转对称性破缺仍以短程纳米尺度区域的形式普遍存在，表明电子向列性与2×2电荷密度波无关。

Abstract: Kagome superconductors $A$V$_3$Sb$_5$ ($A$ = Cs, K, Rb) have developed into an exciting playground for realizing and exploring exotic solid state phenomena. Abundant experimental evidence suggests that electronic structure breaks rotational symmetry of the lattice, but whether this may be a simple consequence of the symmetry of the underlying 2 $\times$ 2 charge density wave phase or an entirely different mechanism remains intensely debated. We use spectroscopic imaging scanning tunneling microscopy to explore the phase diagram of the prototypical kagome superconductor CsV$_3$Sb$_5$ as a function of doping. We intentionally suppress the charge density wave phase with chemical substitutions selectively introduced at two distinct lattice sites, and investigate the resulting system. We discover that rotational symmetry breaking of the electronic structure -- now present in short-range nanoscale regions -- persists in all samples, in a wide doping range long after all charge density waves have been suppressed. As such, our experiments uncover ubiquitous electronic nematicity across the $A$V$_3$Sb$_5$ phase diagram, unrelated to the 2 $\times$ 2 charge density wave. This further points towards electronic nematicity as the intrinsic nature of the parent state of kagome superconductors, under which other exotic low-temperature phenomena subsequently emerge.

Abstract: The doped quantum spin liquid on the kagome lattice provides a fascinating platform to explore exotic quantum states, such as the reported holon Wigner crystal at low doping. On the $L_y=3$ cylinder ($L_y$ is the number of unit cells along the circumference direction), we establish a quantum phase diagram with increasing doping level. In addition to the charge density wave (CDW) states at lower doping, we find an emergent Fermi-liquid-like phase by melting the holon Wigner crystal at $δ\approx 0.15$, which is characterized by suppression of charge density oscillation and power-law decay of various correlation functions. On the wider $L_y = 4$ cylinder, the bond-dimension extrapolated correlation functions also support such a Fermi-liquid-like state, suggesting its stability with increasing system size. In a narrow doping range near $δ= 1/3$ on the $L_y = 3$ cylinder, we find a state with an exponential decay of single-particle correlation but the other correlation functions preserving the features in the Fermi-liquid-like phase, which may be a precursor of a superconducting state. Nevertheless, this peculiar state near $δ= 1/3$ disappears on the $L_y = 4$ cylinder, implying a possible lattice size dependence. Our results reveal a quantum melting from a holon Wigner crystal to a Fermi-liquid-like state with increasing hole density, and suggest a doping regime to explore superconductivity for future study.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了张量重整化算法，该算法专门针对CFT的张量复形结构设计，形成了具有广义对称性的重整化群框架。算法从初级场的三点函数开始，通过重整化流演化出完整的固定点张量。

Result: 即使仅从拓扑数据开始，重整化过程也能重构完整的固定点张量，这种方法被称为"拓扑自举"。这一发现深化了CFT中拓扑方面与动力学方面的联系。

Abstract: Recent progress in generalized symmetry and topological holography has shown that, in conformal field theory (CFT), topological data from one dimensional higher can play a key role in determining local dynamics. Based on this insight, a fixed-point (FP) tensor complex (TC) for CFT has recently been constructed. In this work, we develop a TC renormalization (TCR) algorithm adapted to this CFT-based structure, forming a renormalization-group (RG) framework with generalized symmetry. We show that the full FP tensor can emerge from the RG flow starting with only the three-point function of the primary fields. Remarkably, even when starting solely from topological data, the RG process can still reconstruct the full FP tensor--a method we call as topological bootstrap. This approach deepens the connection between the topological and dynamical aspects of CFT and suggests pathways toward a fully algebraic description of gapless quantum states, with potential extensions to higher dimensions.

Method: 采用无符号问题的投影量子蒙特卡洛算法，研究多种二维二分准晶中半填充Hubbard模型的磁性相。结合对称性分析，提出了判断准晶中Néel态磁性类别的通用判据。

Abstract: Magnetism is a fundamental research area in which the recently proposed altermagnetism (AM) has become an emergent frontier. Very recently, the quasicrystal (QC) was proposed as a possible platform to realize AM. However, the existence of AM in QCs still lacks vigorous evidence. In this work, we adopt the sign-problem-free projector quantum Monte Carlo (PQMC) algorithm to investigate the magnetic phases in the half-filled Hubbard models in various 2D bipartite QCs, and always obtain Néel ordered states. While the Néel states in bipartite crystals are usually antiferromagnetism (AFM), we find it common that those in bipartite QCs can also be AM or ferromagnetism (FM). Based on symmetry analysis, combined with our comprehensive PQMC results, we propose a general criterion for determining the magnetism classes of the Néel states in a bipartite QC: According to whether the two sublattices are related by the inversion, the other point-group operation, or no operation about the unique symmetry center in the QC, the corresponding Néel state is AFM, AM or FM, respectively. For example, our results yield AM for the two $D_4$-symmetric Thue-Morse QCs and FM for the $D_5$-symmetric Penrose QC at half-filling. Our results provide a solid foundation for experimental investigations and potential applications of different classes of magnetism in QCs.

Conclusion: 磁子系统与晶格子系统在脉冲时间尺度（~10⁻¹s）上存在热平衡破坏，表现出异常缓慢的热传递。Nd₂Zr₂O₇中发现了通过磁场变化速率动态控制热流的新机制，为调控材料热动力学行为提供了新途径。

Abstract: We explore the magnetic properties of Nd$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$ and Pr$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$ single crystals subjected to pulsed magnetic fields up to 60 T using magnetization and magnetocaloric-effect (MCE) measurements, with initial temperatures ranging from 2 to 31K. The MCE data exhibit pronounced and unconventional hysteresis loops, in which the sample temperature increases during both the up-sweep and down-sweep of the field. In Nd$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$, the MCE further displays a striking plateau as a function of time, followed by a rapid temperature rise that begins at the maximum applied field, across pulses with differing peak-field strengths. Our magnetization measurements reveal an inferred temperature of the magnetic subsystem that differs significantly from the directly measured sample temperature and exhibits opposite hysteresis: the temperature is higher on the up-sweep than the down-sweep, unlike the direct measurements. These observations indicate a breakdown of thermal equilibrium between magnetic and lattice degrees of freedom on the timescale of the pulse ($\sim 10^{-1}$s). We interpret the results using a phenomenological model involving two thermally coupled subsystems - the magnetic ions and phonons, and a thermal reservoir, which accounts well for the behavior of Pr$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$. However, it fails to reproduce the plateau seen in Nd$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$. Agreement with Nd$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$ data is improved substantially if we allow the thermal coupling between the magnetic and the lattice subsystems to depend on the product $\frac{HdH}{dt}$. Our results reveal anomalously slow heat transfer between magnetic and lattice subsystems and point toward a novel mechanism for dynamically controlling the heat flow in Nd$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$ via the rate of magnetic field variation.

Abstract: Trions, three-body bound states composed of an exciton and an additional charge, are typically fragile and require external excitation to form. Here, we report the spontaneous emergence of a stable trion gas at the surface of the layered semiconductor Ta2NiS5, revealed through angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy. We observe a sharp, highly localized in-gap feature that cannot be explained by conventional band-theory. Instead, we argue that it arises from the formation of negative trions, stabilized by surface-induced band bending and the material's quasi-one-dimensional geometry. Unlike excitons, these trions form without optical pumping and persist at equilibrium, marking a rare example of an interaction-driven surface state in a nominally conventional semiconductor. Our findings establish Ta2NiS5 as a unique platform for exploring many-body physics at surfaces and open new avenues for studying and controlling collective excitations in low-dimensional systems.

### [34] [Electronic Structure and Dynamical Correlations in Antiferromagnetic BiFeO$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23181)
*Yihan Wu,Mario Caserta,Tommaso Chiarotti,Nicola Marzari*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入频率依赖的DFT+U(ω)方法，解决了传统静态Hubbard修正方法在预测反铁磁BiFeO₃电子结构时出现的深价带峰问题，准确再现了实验观测的光电子谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统静态Hubbard修正方法（DFT+U、DFT+U+V）在预测反铁磁BiFeO₃电子结构时，错误地预测了深价带Fe 3d峰（约-7 eV），与硬X射线光电子能谱实验观测相矛盾。这促使研究者探索更准确的动态关联方法。

Method: 采用频率依赖的DFT+U(ω)方法和动态Hubbard泛函（dynH）。通过自旋极化RPA计算屏蔽库仑相互作用U(ω)，投影到最大局域化的Fe 3d Wannier轨道上，表示为极点求和形式，产生增强Kohn-Sham哈密顿量的自能。

Result: DFT+U(ω)方法预测了1.53 eV的基本带隙，与实验一致，并完全消除了不合理的深价带峰。模拟的HAXPES谱与实验线形吻合，精度达到或超过了计算要求更高的DFT+DMFT方法。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了动态屏蔽在复杂氧化物中的关键作用，并确立了DFT+U(ω)作为一种预测性强、计算效率高的关联材料计算方法。

Abstract: We study the electronic structure and dynamical correlations in antiferromagnetic BiFeO$_3$, a prototypical room-temperature multiferroic, using a variety of static and dynamical first-principles methods. Conventional static Hubbard corrections (DFT+$U$, DFT+$U$+$V$) incorrectly predict a deep-valence Fe $3d$ peak (around $-7\,\text{eV}$) in antiferromagnetic BiFeO$_3$, in contradiction with hard-X-ray photoemission. We resolve this failure by using a recent generalization of DFT+$U$ to include a frequency-dependent screening -- DFT+$U(ω)$ -- or using a dynamical Hubbard functional (dynH). The screened Coulomb interaction $U(ω)$, computed with spin-polarized RPA and projected onto maximally localized Fe $3d$ Wannier orbitals, is expressed as a sum-over-poles, yielding a self-energy that augments the Kohn--Sham Hamiltonian. This DFT+$U(ω)$ approach predicts a fundamental band gap of $1.53\,\text{eV}$, consistent with experiments, and completely eliminates the unphysical deep-valence peak. The resulting simulated HAXPES spectrum reproduces the experimental lineshape with an accuracy matching or exceeding that of far more demanding DFT+DMFT calculations. Our work demonstrates the critical nature of dynamical screening in complex oxides and establishes DFT+$U(ω)$ as a predictive, computationally efficient method for correlated materials.

### [36] [On the $2$-torsion in class groups of number fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21899)
*Dante Bonolis*

Main category: math.NT

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bhargava等人在2020年证明了对于次数n≥5的有限扩张K/Q，2-挠类群的大小有上界O_{n,ε}(D_K^{1/2-1/2n+ε})。本文旨在改进这一上界，获得更紧的估计。

Method: 通过引入新的常数δ_K ≥ 1/(28n) - 3/(28n(n-1))，改进了原有的指数估计方法，使得上界指数进一步降低。

Result: 证明了#h_2(K) = O_{n,ε}(D_K^{1/2-1/2n-δ_K+ε})，其中δ_K ≥ 1/(28n) - 3/(28n(n-1))，这比Bhargava等人的结果更优。

Conclusion: 本文成功改进了数域2-挠类群大小的上界估计，为相关数论问题提供了更精确的理论工具。

Abstract: In $2020$, Bhargava, Shankar, Taniguchi, Thorne, Tsimerman, and Zhao proved that for a finite extension $K/\mathbb{Q}$ of degree $n\geq 5$, the size of the $2$-torsion class group is bounded by $\# h_{2}(K)=O_{n,\varepsilon}(D_{K}^{\frac{1}{2}-\frac{1}{2n}+\varepsilon})$, where $D_{K}$ is the absolute discriminant of $K$. In the present paper, we improve their bound by proving that $\# h_{2}(K)=O_{n,\varepsilon}(D_{K}^{\frac{1}{2}-\frac{1}{2n}-δ_{K}+\varepsilon})$, for a constant $δ_{K}\geq\frac{1}{28n}-\frac{3}{28n(n-1)}$.

### [37] [An analogue of Kida's formula for Mazur-Tate elements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21979)
*Naman Pratap,Anwesh Ray*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 该论文证明了椭圆曲线上Mazur-Tate元素的Iwasawa不变量满足Kida公式的类似结果，统一了此前所有已知的解析Iwasawa不变量Kida公式情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究椭圆曲线上Mazur-Tate元素的Iwasawa不变量在数域扩张中的变化规律，特别是在p-幂伽罗瓦扩张中μ-不变量的保持性和λ-不变量的显式转移公式，以统一此前关于Selmer群和p进L函数的Kida公式结果。

Method: 研究椭圆曲线E/Q在数域K和L（具有p-幂伽罗瓦群）的有限层上的Mazur-Tate元素，其中L/K是阿贝尔数域的伽罗瓦扩张。证明μ-不变量在扩张中保持：如果K上的n级Mazur-Tate元素μ=0，则L上的对应元素也有μ=0，并推导出λ-不变量的显式转移公式。

Result: 证明了Mazur-Tate元素的μ-不变量在p-幂伽罗瓦扩张中保持为零，并得到了λ-不变量的显式转移公式。应用这一结果，获得了Pollack符号p进L函数和Delbourgo构造的不稳定加性约化椭圆曲线p进L函数的Kida型公式。

Conclusion: 该研究统一了所有已知的解析Iwasawa不变量Kida公式情况，由于Mazur-Tate元素在极限中逼近p进L函数，这一结果为椭圆曲线在各种约化类型（包括加性约化）下的Iwasawa理论提供了统一的框架。

Abstract: We prove an analogue of Kida's formula for the Iwasawa invariants of the Mazur-Tate elements attached to elliptic curves over $\mathbb{Q}$. Let $p$ be an odd prime and let $L/K$ be a Galois extension of abelian number fields with $p$-power Galois group. For an elliptic curve $E/\mathbb{Q}$, we study the Mazur-Tate elements over the finite layers of the cyclotomic $\mathbb{Z}_p$-extensions of $K$ and $L$. We show that the vanishing of the $μ$-invariant is preserved in the extension: if the level-$n$ Mazur-Tate element over $K$ has $μ= 0$, then the corresponding element over $L$ also has $μ= 0$. Moreover, the associated $λ$-invariants satisfy an explicit transition formula. This parallels the work of Hachimori-Matsuno on Selmer groups and of Matsuno on $p$-adic $L$-functions. As an application, we obtain an analogue of Kida's formula for the analytic Iwasawa invariants associated to Pollack's signed $p$-adic $L$-functions. Since our results apply to elliptic curves with any reduction type at $p$ under mild hypotheses, including those with additive reduction, we also obtain a Kida-type formula for the $p$-adic $L$-functions constructed by Delbourgo for elliptic curves with unstable additive reduction. In particular, because Mazur-Tate elements approximate $p$-adic $L$-functions in the limit, our results unify all previously known cases of Kida's formula for analytic Iwasawa invariants.

In particular, we obtain a subconvexity bound when $π_1\otimesπ_2$ stays uniformly away from QUE-like case. ### [40] [Zeta Spectral Triples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22755)
*Alain Connes,Caterina Consani,Henri Moscovici*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于谱实现证明黎曼猜想的新策略，通过构造自伴算子来逼近黎曼ζ函数的非平凡零点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为黎曼猜想提供一种新的证明途径，通过谱理论方法将ζ函数的零点问题转化为自伴算子的谱分析问题。

Method: 构造自伴算子作为标度算子谱三元组的秩一扰动，仅涉及素数p≤x=λ²的欧拉乘积，利用Toeplitz矩阵的Carathéodory-Fejer定理保证自伴性。

Result: 数值实验显示算子谱与ζ(1/2+is)的最低非平凡零点高度吻合，即使对于较小的x值；正则化行列式收敛于黎曼Ξ函数。

Conclusion: 该构造为黎曼猜想提供了潜在的证明框架，算子谱收敛于ζ函数零点将直接证明黎曼猜想，正则化行列式在分析中起关键作用。

Abstract: We propose and investigate a strategy toward a proof of the Riemann Hypothesis based on a spectral realization of its non-trivial zeros. Our approach constructs self-adjoint operators obtained as rank-one perturbations of the spectral triple associated with the scaling operator on the interval $[λ^{-1}, λ]$. The construction only involves the Euler products over the primes $p \leq x = λ^2$ and produces self-adjoint operators whose spectra coincide, with striking numerical accuracy, with the lowest non-trivial zeros of $ζ(1/2 + i s)$, even for small values of $x$.
  The theoretical foundation rests on the framework introduced in "Spectral triples and zeta-cycles" (Enseign. Math. 69 (2023), no. 1-2, 93-148), together with the extension in "Quadratic Forms, Real Zeros and Echoes of the Spectral Action" (Commun. Math. Phys. (2025)) of the classical Caratheodory-Fejer theorem for Toeplitz matrices, which guarantees the necessary self-adjointness.
  Numerical experiments show that the spectra of the operators converge towards the zeros of $ζ(1/2 + i s)$ as the parameters $N, λ\to \infty$. A rigorous proof of this convergence would establish the Riemann Hypothesis. We further compute the regularized determinants of these operators and discuss the analytic role they play in controlling and potentially proving the above result by showing that, suitably normalized, they converge towards the Riemann $Ξ$ function.

</details>


### [41] [Splitting p-primary cohomology classes of tori in characteristic p](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22797)
*Zev Rosengarten*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 证明了在全局函数域上，环面T的p-主上同调类可以通过合适的可分p-主扩张分裂，并给出了分裂扩张的度上界


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究全局函数域上环面的上同调类分裂问题，特别是p-主上同调类在可分扩张中的行为

Method: 使用"大"p-主扩张分裂上同调类，证明Grunwald-Wang类型结果来逼近局部扩张，并构造具体的可分p-主扩张

Result: p-主上同调类可以在"大"p-主扩张中分裂，p^n-挠类可以通过度≤(p^n)^{1+cm log(m)^3}的可分p-主扩张分裂，其中c是可计算的通用常数

Conclusion: 在全局函数域上，环面的p-主上同调类可以通过可控度的可分p-主扩张分裂，相关方法具有独立意义的Grunwald-Wang类型结果

Abstract: We prove that $p$-primary cohomology classes of a torus $T$ over a global function field of characteristic $p$ may be split by suitable separable $p$-primary extensions. More precisely, we show that such cohomology classes will split in any ``large'' $p$-primary extension (and in fact, prove the same for $\ell$-primary classes over ``large'' $\ell$-primary extensions for every prime $\ell$, including $\ell \neq \mathrm{char}(K)$), and we prove that $p^n$-torsion classes may be split by a (solvable) separable $p$-primary extension of degree $\leq (p^n)^{1+cm\mathrm{log}(m)^3}$ for an explicitly computable universal constant $c > 0$, where $m$ is the degree of a finite Galois extension splitting the torus $T$. Along the way, we also prove Grunwald-Wang type results of independent interest which allow one to approximate a given finite list of abelian $p$-primary local extensions of places of a global function field by a suitable global extension.

</details>

Furthermore, we analyze the $p$-adic distribution of these groups in the moduli space of filtered $\varphi$-modules. ### [43] [Eventual periodicity of the Smith forms of integer matrix powers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22814)
*Vanni Noferini*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 证明了整数方阵幂的Smith形式具有最终周期性：存在n₀和T，使得当n≥n₀时，SF(A^{n+T}) = D·SF(A^n)，其中D是常数对角矩阵


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决R. Bruner在2013年提出的猜想，研究整数矩阵幂的Smith形式的渐近行为

Method: 通过数学证明方法，分析整数矩阵幂的Smith形式的周期性特征，建立理论框架证明最终周期性

Result: 证明了整数矩阵幂的Smith形式具有最终周期性，即存在n₀、T和常数对角矩阵D，使得当n≥n₀时，SF(A^{n+T}) = D·SF(A^n)，并且n₀和T可以任意大

Conclusion: 该研究为R. Bruner的猜想提供了最终肯定的答案，揭示了整数矩阵幂的Smith形式的渐近周期性行为，对代数数论和矩阵理论有重要意义

Abstract: We prove that the Smith forms of the powers of an integer square matrix behave in an eventually periodic manner. More precisely, if $\mathrm{SF}(M)$ denotes the Smith form of $M \in \Z^{m \times m}$, then for every $A \in \Z^{m \times m}$ there exist $n_0 \in \N$, an integer $T \geq 1$, and a constant diagonal matrix $D \in \Z^{m \times m}$ such that $n \geq n_0$ implies $\mathrm{SF}(A^{n+T})=D \cdot \mathrm{SF}(A^n)$. This provides an eventually affirmative answer to a conjecture posed in 2013 by R. Bruner. We also show that both $n_0$ and $T$ can be arbitrarily large.

</details>

Method: 利用Einsiedler和Lindenstrauss的测度刚性结果，证明相关秩一adelic环面束上均匀测度极限的熵大于最大熵的一半，结合Siegel质量公式和Bombieri-Pila以及Heath-Brown发展的行列式方法

Based on this, it suffices to show that limits of the uniform measures on the associated rank one adelic toral packets have more entropy than one half of the maximal entropy. ### [45] [The Structure and Degrees of Polynomials Computing Square Roots $\mod p$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22881)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当p≡3 mod 4时，计算平方根的多项式f(X)=X^{(p+1)/4}是已知的最小次数多项式。但当p≡1 mod 4时，情况不明确，虽然Tonelli-Shanks算法可以构造这样的多项式，但其是否具有最小次数仍是一个开放问题。

Method: 研究计算平方根的多项式的各种次数和结构，分析Tonelli-Shanks算法构造的多项式，并探讨是否存在更小次数的多项式。

Conclusion: 对于p≡1 mod 4的情况，计算平方根的最小次数多项式问题仍未完全解决，需要进一步研究来确定Tonelli-Shanks算法构造的多项式是否确实是最优的。

Abstract: For an odd prime $p$, we say a polynomial $f\in \mathbb F_p[X]$ computes square roots if $f(a)^2=a$ for all nonzero, perfect squares $a\in \mathbb F_p$. When $p\equiv 3 \mod 4$, it is easy to see that $f(X)=X^{\frac{p+1}{4}}$ is the smallest such polynomial. For $p\equiv 1 \mod 4$, the situation is less clear. Tonelli-Shanks offers an algorithm for constructing polynomials that compute square roots, but the question of whether their degree is minimal remains. In this paper, we study the various degrees and structures of polynomials computing square roots.

</details>

Abstract: We study the average shifted convolution sum $$ B(H,N):= \frac{1}{H} \sum_{h \sim H} \sum_{n \sim N} A_{π_1}(n)\, A_{π_2}(n+h), $$ where $A_{π_i}(n)$ denotes the Fourier coefficients of a Hecke--Maass cusp form $π_i$ for $SL(d_i,\mathbb{Z})$ with $d_i\ge 4$, $i=1,2$. For the cases $d_1 = d_2 + 1$ and $d_1 = d_2$, we establish a nontrivial power-saving bound of $B(H,N)$ for the range of the shift $H\ge N^{1-\frac{4}{d_1+d_2}+\varepsilon}$ for any $\varepsilon>0$, extending beyond the results of Friedlander and Iwaniec. In particular, when $d_1 = d_2$, we reach the critical threshold $H\ge N^{1-2/d+\varepsilon}$ such that any further improvement in this range yields a subconvexity bound for the corresponding standard $L$-function in the $t$-aspect.

*Elisa Bellah,Claire Dunn,Vernon Naidu,Alette Wells*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 该论文研究Markoff方程X²+Y²+Z²=3XYZ的模p解提升问题，通过分析Vieta群作用下的图连通性，利用Fibonacci序列的Pisano周期结果，特别针对p+1有较大2-adic赋值的素数，证明了对于满足特定条件的Mersenne素数，特殊点(1,1,1)位于已知的连通分量中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Markoff方程是否满足每个模p解都能提升为整数解的特殊Diophantine性质猜想。该猜想与Vieta群在模p非零解上的作用图的连通性密切相关。

Method: 利用Fibonacci序列的Pisano周期结果，分析Vieta群作用在Markoff方程模p解上的图结构。特别关注p+1具有较大2-adic赋值的素数情况，特别是Mersenne素数。

Result: 对于满足p ≡ ±2 (mod 5)的Mersenne素数，证明了特殊点(1,1,1)（在模p约化下固定）位于图中已知的连通分量中。这为Markoff方程的模p解提升猜想提供了新的进展。

Conclusion: 通过结合Fibonacci序列的Pisano周期理论和图连通性分析，为Markoff方程的特殊Diophantine性质猜想提供了新的证据，特别是在特定类型的Mersenne素数情况下取得了明确结果。

Abstract: It is conjectured that the Markoff equation $X^2+Y^2+Z^2=3XYZ$ satisfies the special Diophantine property that every mod $p$ solution lifts to an integer solution. Progress toward this conjecture has been made by studying the connectedness of the graphs obtained from the action of the Vieta group on the nonzero mod $p$ solutions to the Markoff equation. In this paper, we use results on Pisano periods of the Fibonacci sequence to obtain explicit results on the connectedness of special points in this graph for primes $p$ where $p+1$ has large $2$-adic valuation. In particular, for Mersenne primes $p \equiv \pm 2 \,(\text{mod}\, 5)$, we show that the special point $(1, 1, 1)$ which is fixed under reduction modulo $p$ lies in a component of this graph which is known to be connected.

</details>

### [53] [Bayesian Risk-averse Model Predictive Control with Consistency and Stability Guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21871)
*Yingke Li,Yifan Lin,Enlu Zhou,Fumin Zhang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个贝叶斯风险规避模型预测控制框架，用于处理在线学习模型不确定性的随机非线性系统，通过分离认知不确定性和偶然不确定性，并提供贝叶斯学习一致性和闭环稳定性的理论保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模型预测控制（MPC）在约束控制中很强大，但当预测模型在线学习时，其性能和安全会受到模型不确定性的严重影响。需要开发一个能够提供理论保证的框架来处理这种不确定性。

Method: 1. 研究反馈控制诱导的条件独立状态转移下的贝叶斯学习，建立无限可数参数空间上的贝叶斯一致性条件
2. 引入基于比较函数类的风险规避渐近稳定性（RAAS）概念，推导风险规避李雅普诺夫稳定性定理和MPC特定稳定性条件
3. 设计贝叶斯风险规避MPC方案，分离认知（参数）和偶然（扰动）不确定性：扰动以风险中性方式处理，参数不确定性通过动态收缩的模糊集管理，使用粒子滤波在线近似贝叶斯可信区间
4. 提出最优和次优的滚动时域控制策略，次优策略通过从前一解热启动获得

Result: 建立了贝叶斯学习在反馈控制下的理论一致性条件，推导了风险规避渐近稳定性的通用框架，设计了实用的贝叶斯风险规避MPC方案，并证明了当贝叶斯估计器变得一致时，可以恢复渐近RAAS。

Conclusion: 该工作为在线学习模型不确定性的随机非线性系统提供了一个具有理论保证的贝叶斯风险规避MPC框架，通过分离不确定性类型和动态调整模糊集，实现了性能与安全的平衡，并提供了实时实现的可行性。

Abstract: Model Predictive Control (MPC) is a powerful framework for constrained control, but its performance and safety can be severely degraded when the prediction model is learned online and thus remains uncertain. In this work, we develop a Bayesian risk-averse MPC framework for stochastic, discrete-time, nonlinear systems that provides theoretical guarantees on the consistency of Bayesian learning and closed-loop stability. First, we study Bayesian learning under the conditionally independent state transitions induced by feedback control and establish explicit conditions for Bayesian consistency on an infinitely countable parameter space. Second, we introduce a general notion of risk-averse asymptotic stability (RAAS), defined via comparison function classes and independent of any specific coherent risk measure or convergence rate, and we derive a risk-averse Lyapunov stability theorem together with MPC-specific stability conditions. Third, building on these foundations, we design a practical Bayesian risk-averse MPC scheme that separates epistemic (parametric) and aleatoric (disturbance) uncertainty: additive disturbances are treated in a risk-neutral fashion, while parametric uncertainty is managed via dynamically shrinking ambiguity sets constructed from Bayesian credible intervals, approximated online using particle filtering. To enable real-time implementation, we propose both an optimal and a sub-optimal receding-horizon control policy, the latter obtained by warm-starting from the previous solution, and prove that asymptotic RAAS is recovered as the Bayesian estimator becomes consistent.

Method: 提出了一种两步步长调度策略，将确定性优化中著名的两步银步长调度从确定性设置推广到随机优化场景。该方法考虑了随机梯度的方差界限与初始最优性间隙的比值关系。

We consider the setting where only stochastic gradient approximations, which are unbiased, of bounded variance, and supported on a finite set, are accessible. When the variance bound is relatively smaller than a ratio of the initial optimality gap, the proposed stepsize schedule achieves better convergence performance compared to the well-regarded constant stepsize α = 2/(M+m), where m and M denote the strong convexity and gradient-Lipschitz parameters, respectively. Our stepsize schedule can be viewed as a generalization of the well-known two-step silver stepsize schedule in [J. M. Altschuler and P. A. Parrilo, Journal of the ACM, 72(2):1-38, 2025] from deterministic setting to stochastic optimization.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用尖峰变分技术处理非凸控制域问题，引入二阶伴随过程推导必要的最大值原理。针对由均值场机制转换奇异随机微分方程描述的系统，建立理论框架并推导必要和充分的奇异随机最大值原理。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate a mean-field singular stochastic optimal control problem for systems governed by mean-field regime-switching singular stochastic differential equations. The state process is assumed to depend on both a regular and a singular control, and the coefficient associated with the singular component is allowed to be regime dependent. We derive both necessary and sufficient singular stochastic maximum principles. Because the regular control domain is not assumed to be convex, we employ the spike variation technique and obtain the necessary maximum principle by introducing a second-order adjoint process. As an application, we use the main theoretical results to analyse an inter-bank borrowing and lending model with transaction costs.

### [56] [A nonmonotone extrapolated proximal gradient-subgradient algorithm beyond global Lipschitz gradient continuity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22011)
*Lei Yang,Jingjing Hu,Tianxiang Liu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代应用中越来越多的复合优化问题不具有全局Lipschitz连续梯度，这阻碍了传统PG方法的使用。虽然已有研究开始探索无需迭代有界性假设的收敛分析，但如何设计更高效算法仍是一个开放问题。

Method: 提出了一种问题参数无关算法，包含精心设计的非单调线搜索来处理非全局Lipschitz梯度连续性，并结合外推步骤以实现潜在加速。算法在KL性质下建立了收敛分析，无需迭代有界性假设。

Result: 建立了算法在Kurdyka-Łojasiewicz性质下的收敛性分析，无需任何迭代有界性假设。数值实验验证了算法的有效性，并展示了结合外推与非单调线搜索的优势。

Abstract: With the advancement of modern applications, an increasing number of composite optimization problems arise whose smooth component does not possess a globally Lipschitz continuous gradient. This setting prevents the direct use of the proximal gradient (PG) method and its variants, and has motivated a growing body of research on new PG-type methods and their convergence theory, in particular, global convergence analysis without imposing any explicit or implicit boundedness assumptions on the iterates. Until recently, the first complete analysis of this kind has been established for the PG method and its specific nonmonotone variants, which has since stimulated further exploration along this research direction. In this paper, we consider a general composite optimization model beyond the global Lipschitz gradient continuity setting. We propose a novel problem-parameter-free algorithm that incorporates a carefully designed nonmonotone line search to handle the non-global Lipschitz gradient continuity, together with an extrapolation step to achieve potential acceleration. Despite the added technical challenges introduced by combining extrapolation with nonmonotone line search, we establish a refined convergence analysis for the proposed algorithm under the Kurdyka-Ł ojasiewicz property, without requiring any boundedness assumptions on the iterates. This work thus further advances the theoretical understanding of PG-type methods in the non-global Lipschitz gradient continuity setting. Finally, we conduct numerical experiments to illustrate the effectiveness of our algorithm and highlight the advantages of integrating extrapolation with a nonmonotone line search.

  <summary>Details</summary>

By leveraging reduced-order modeling, the method enables real-time control in high-dimensional flow environments. Simulations demonstrate accurate flow-field reconstruction and efficient trajectory generation within realistic wind environments.

### [58] [A Two-Stage Stochastic Optimization Framework for Environmentally Sensitive Oil Spill Response Resource Allocation in the Arctic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22218)
*Md Ashiqur Rahman,Mustofa Tanbir Kuhel,Clara Novoa*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个两阶段随机混合整数线性规划框架，用于优化阿拉斯加北极地区溢油应急站的选址和资源分配，考虑了多种不确定性因素，相比确定性方法提高了35.45%的应急效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着气候变化导致海冰消退，阿拉斯加北极地区海上交通增加，溢油风险成为紧迫的环境和后勤问题。传统的确定性应急规划模型无法处理关键的不确定性因素，如溢油量变化、环境敏感性变化和基础设施限制。

Method: 开发了一个两阶段随机混合整数线性规划框架，联合优化溢油应急站的位置和异构资源在多概率溢油情景下的分配。模型整合了加权目标函数，包括溢油量、环境敏感性指数、响应时间以及站点设置、部署和站间转移成本。使用Gurobi优化器求解，并对324种重要性和生态权重组合进行敏感性分析。

Result: 结果显示，相比确定性方法，响应效果提高了约35.45%（通过随机解的价值确认）。敏感性分析揭示了成本和生态覆盖之间的明确权衡关系。模型为北极应急规划者提供了数据驱动的决策支持工具。

Conclusion: 该框架为北极应急规划者提供了一个数据驱动的决策支持工具，能够同时考虑不确定性、环境敏感性和现实的后勤约束，在生态保护和运营效率之间实现平衡。

Abstract: The risk of oil spills in the Alaskan Arctic has become an urgent environmental and logistical concern as maritime traffic increases under climate driven sea ice retreat. Traditional deterministic response planning models fail to represent key uncertainties, including variable spill magnitudes, changing environmental sensitivity, and infrastructure limitations. This study develops a two-stage stochastic mixed integer linear programming framework that jointly optimizes the location of oil spill response stations and the allocation of heterogeneous resources across multiple probabilistic spill scenarios. The model integrates a weighted objective that combines spill volume, environmental sensitivity index (ESI), response time, and costs for station setup, deployment, and inter station transfer. Separate importance weights for coverage and cost, together with internal ecological weights, allow decision makers to balance ecological protection and operational efficiency. Data was compiled from Alaska Department of Environmental Conservation spill records and National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration ESI layers and are converted into model ready scenarios through harmonization and sampling. The model is solved with the Gurobi optimizer, and sensitivity analysis is performed over 324 combinations of importance and ecological weights. Results show about a 35.45% percent improvement in response effectiveness over deterministic methods, as confirmed by the value of the stochastic solution, and reveal clear tradeoffs between cost and ecological coverage. The framework provides a data driven decision support tool for Arctic emergency planners that simultaneously accounts for uncertainty, environmental sensitivity, and realistic logistical constraints.

### [59] [A Framework for Handling and Exploiting Symmetry in Benders' Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22251)
*Christopher Hojny,Cédric Roy*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文开发了Benders分解框架中的对称性处理理论，通过构建特殊图结构检测对称性，并设计了对称Benders割的分离和聚合技术，显著减少了分离oracle的执行次数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Benders分解是解决优化问题的重要框架，但其中一直缺乏系统性的对称性处理技术。主要原因是Benders割不是显式已知的，而是通过分离oracle生成的，这使得传统的对称性处理方法难以应用。

Method: 1. 开发了BD框架中的对称性检测理论，引入了一类特殊的图结构来捕捉Benders主问题和Benders oracle的对称性信息；2. 一旦通过现有技术找到这些图的对称性，就可以应用经典的对称性处理方法加速BD；3. 设计了对称Benders割的分离和聚合技术，包括定制的分离程序和扩展公式，大幅减少了分离oracle的执行次数。

Result: 在装箱和调度问题的数值研究中，验证了对称性处理和割聚合技术的有效性，表明这些方法能够显著提高Benders分解的求解效率。

Conclusion: 本研究填补了Benders分解框架中对称性处理的空白，通过理论创新和算法设计，使得对称性处理技术能够系统性地应用于BD框架，为优化问题的求解提供了新的加速手段。

Abstract: Benders' decomposition (BD) is a framework for solving optimization problems by removing some variables and modeling their contribution to the original problem via so-called Benders cuts. While many advanced optimization techniques can be applied in a BD framework, one central technique has not been applied systematically in BD: symmetry handling. The main reason for this is that Benders cuts are not known explicitly but only generated via a separation oracle.
  In this work, we close this gap by developing a theory of symmetry detection within the BD framework. To this end, we introduce a tailored family of graphs that capture the symmetry information of both the Benders master problem and the Benders oracles. Once symmetries of these graphs are known, which can be found by established techniques, classical symmetry handling approaches become available to accelerate BD. We complement these approaches by devising techniques for the separation and aggregation of symmetric Benders cuts by means of tailored separation routines and extended formulations. Both substantially reduce the number of executions of the separation oracles. In a numerical study, we show the effect of both symmetry handling and cut aggregation for bin packing and scheduling problems.

</details>


### [60] [On the Condition Number Dependency in Bilevel Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22331)
*Lesi Chen,Jingzhao Zhang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文研究了双层优化问题的oracle复杂度，针对上层非凸、下层强凸的情况，建立了新的下界Ω(κ²ε⁻²)和上界Õ(κ⁷/²ε⁻²)，首次证明了双层问题与极小极大问题在此设置下的复杂度差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对双层优化问题的oracle复杂度已有Õ(κ⁴ε⁻²)的上界结果，但关于条件数κ的最优依赖关系尚不清楚。本文旨在确定双层优化问题在oracle复杂度上相对于条件数κ的最优依赖关系，并揭示其与极小极大问题的本质差异。

Method: 通过理论分析建立新的复杂度下界和上界。首先构造反例证明Ω(κ²ε⁻²)的下界，然后设计算法实现Õ(κ⁷/²ε⁻²)的上界。方法扩展到多种设置：高阶光滑函数、随机oracle和凸超目标函数。

Result: 1. 建立了Ω(κ²ε⁻²)的下界和Õ(κ⁷/²ε⁻²)的上界，首次证明双层问题与极小极大问题存在复杂度差距；2. 对于二阶和任意光滑问题，分别得到Ω(κ_y^{13/4}ε^{-12/7})和Ω(κ^{17/10}ε^{-8/5})下界；3. 对于凸-强凸问题，将下界从Ω(κ/√ε)改进到Ω(κ^{5/4}/√ε)；4. 对于光滑随机问题，得到Ω(κ⁴ε⁻⁴)下界。

Conclusion: 本文首次建立了双层优化问题在oracle复杂度上关于条件数κ的明确下界和上界，证明了双层问题比极小极大问题更难优化。这些结果为理解双层优化的计算复杂性提供了理论基础，并为算法设计提供了指导。

Abstract: Bilevel optimization minimizes an objective function, defined by an upper-level problem whose feasible region is the solution of a lower-level problem. We study the oracle complexity of finding an $ε$-stationary point with first-order methods when the upper-level problem is nonconvex and the lower-level problem is strongly convex. Recent works (Ji et al., ICML 2021; Arbel and Mairal, ICLR 2022; Chen el al., JMLR 2025) achieve a $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(κ^4 ε^{-2})$ upper bound that is near-optimal in $ε$. However, the optimal dependency on the condition number $κ$ is unknown. In this work, we establish a new $Ω(κ^2 ε^{-2})$ lower bound and $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(κ^{7/2} ε^{-2})$ upper bound for this problem, establishing the first provable gap between bilevel problems and minimax problems in this setup. Our lower bounds can be extended to various settings, including high-order smooth functions, stochastic oracles, and convex hyper-objectives: (1) For second-order and arbitrarily smooth problems, we show $Ω(κ_y^{13/4} ε^{-12/7})$ and $Ω(κ^{17/10} ε^{-8/5})$ lower bounds, respectively. (2) For convex-strongly-convex problems, we improve the previously best lower bound (Ji and Liang, JMLR 2022) from $Ω(κ/\sqrtε)$ to $Ω(κ^{5/4} / \sqrtε)$. (3) For smooth stochastic problems, we show an $Ω(κ^4 ε^{-4})$ lower bound.

</details>


### [61] [A Variational Approach to Mean Field Type Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22428)
*Alain Bensoussan,Ziyu Huang,Sheung Chi Phillip Yam*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 该论文将变分方法从经典随机控制扩展到平均场控制理论，通过研究HJB方程而非HJ-FP耦合系统，为平均场控制提供了新的视角和方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统平均场控制理论采用HJ-FP耦合系统方法，而变分方法在经典随机控制中已有成功应用。作者希望将变分方法扩展到平均场控制，作为现有方法的替代方案，以处理更广泛的平均场控制问题。

Method: 采用变分方法研究平均场控制中的HJB方程，而非传统的HJ-FP耦合系统或主方程。该方法对系数的正则性要求较低，具有中等正则性即可。

Result: 成功将变分方法应用于平均场控制理论，能够解决更广泛的平均场控制问题，为概率方法提供了新的视角，且对系数正则性要求较少。

Conclusion: 变分方法为平均场控制理论提供了有效的替代方案，能够处理更广泛的问题类别，且对正则性条件要求较低，为相关研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Variational methods have been used to study stochastic control for long, see Bensoussan (1982) and Bensoussan-Lions (1978) for the early works. More precisely, variational approaches apply to the study of Bellman equation as a parabolic quasi-linear equation, when the nonlinearity affects only the gradient of the solution, and the second order derivative term is linear and not degenerate. This corresponds to a stochastic control problem, where the state equation is a diffusion process. The primary objective of this article is to extend this approach to mean field control theory, as an alternative to the current approach, which considers a coupled system of Hamilton-Jacobi (HJ) and Fokker-Planck (FP) equations, since the introduction of the theory by Lasry-Lions (2007). The main novelty lies in that the equation studied here is the HJB equation, neither the HJ-FP system nor the master equation; and our results also provide another perspective for probabilistic approaches; see Chassagneux-Crisan-Delarue (2022), Bensoussan-Wong-Yam-Yuan (2024), Bensoussan-Tai-Yam (2025) and Bensoussan-Huang-Tang-Yam (2025) for instance. Within the scope of the PDE methods, the advantage of this article is to solve a larger class of mean field control problems, with moderate regularity; and this kind of variational methods fairly require few conditions on the regularity of the coefficients.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有逆最优控制方法在噪声和非线性设置下存在估计器的一致性问题，需要开发能够保证统计一致性的新方法。

Abstract: Inverse Optimal Control (IOC) seeks to recover an unknown cost from expert demonstrations, and it provides a systematic way of modeling experts' decision mechanisms while considering the prior information of the cost functions. Nevertheless, existing IOC methods have consistency issue with the estimator under noisy and nonlinear settings. In this paper, we consider a discrete-time nonlinear system with process noise, and it is controlled by an optimal policy that minimizes the expectation of a discounted cumulative cost function across an infinite time-horizon. In particular, the cost function takes the form of a linear combination of a priori known feature functions. In this setting, we first adopt Lasserre's reformulation of the forward problem with occupancy measure. Next, we propose the infinite dimensional IOC algorithm and further approximate it with Lagrange interpolating polynomials, which results in a convex, finite-dimensional sum-of-squares optimization. Moreover, the estimator is shown to be asymptotically and statistically consistent. Finally, we validate the theoretical results and illustrate the performance of our method with numerical experiments. In addition, the robustness and generalizability performance of the proposed IOC algorithm are also illustrated.

### [63] [Variational analysis of determinantal varieties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22613)
*Yan Yang,Bin Gao,Ya-xiang Yuan*

Main category: math.OC

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低秩集合（行列式簇）在低秩优化中受到广泛关注，但其二阶几何结构（曲率信息）比一阶切锥更为复杂。现有研究缺乏统一的框架来处理各种低秩集合的几何结构，特别是二阶切集的计算。

Method: 开发统一框架推导低秩集合的一阶和二阶切集显式公式；框架可处理低秩集合与其他集合的交集，得到切交集规则；通过切集视角分析非光滑问题与其光滑参数化的二阶驻点等价性；研究矩阵簇法锥图的变分几何，推导其Bouligand切锥、Fréchet和Mordukhovich法锥。

Conclusion: 该框架统一处理了低秩集合的几何分析，为低秩优化提供了理论基础；切集方法有助于理解优化问题的几何结构；二阶最优性验证的NP难性揭示了低秩优化的计算复杂性；法锥图几何结果扩展了双层规划的最优性理论。

Abstract: Determinantal varieties -- the sets of bounded-rank matrices or tensors -- have attracted growing interest in low-rank optimization. The tangent cone to low-rank sets is widely studied and underpins a range of geometric methods. The second-order geometry, which encodes curvature information, is more intricate. In this work, we develop a unified framework to derive explicit formulas for both first- and second-order tangent sets to various low-rank sets, including low-rank matrices, tensors, symmetric matrices, and positive semidefinite matrices. The framework also accommodates the intersection of a low-rank set and another set satisfying mild assumptions, thereby yielding a tangent intersection rule. Through the lens of tangent sets, we establish a necessary and sufficient condition under which a nonsmooth problem and its smooth parameterization share equivalent second-order stationary points. Moreover, we exploit tangent sets to characterize optimality conditions for low-rank optimization and prove that verifying second-order optimality is NP-hard. In a separate line of analysis, we investigate variational geometry of the graph of the normal cone to matrix varieties, deriving the explicit Bouligand tangent cone, Fréchet and Mordukhovich normal cones to the graph. These results are further applied to develop optimality conditions for low-rank bilevel programs.

Abstract: A multi-variable adaptive controller is derived as the explicit solution to a minimax dynamic game. The maximizing player selects disturbances and model parameters for the underlying linear time-invariant dynamics. This leads to a Bellman equation that can be solved explicitly for the case with unitary B-matrix known up to a sign and no input penalty. The minimizing policy is a dual controller that optimizes the tradeoff between exploration and exploitation.

Abstract: Evaluating the reliability of machine learning classifications remains a fundamental challenge in Artificial Intelligence (AI), particularly when the target variable is multidimensional. Classification variables can be expressed by means of a categorical scale which, at best, is ordinal. Because ordinal data lack a natural metric structure in their underlying space, most conventional distance measures aimed at assessing the accuracy of machine learning classifications cannot be directly or meaningfully applied. In this paper, we develop a mathematical framework for comparing ordinal data based on a family of Rank Graduation $(\mathrm{RGX}_p)$ \emph{metrics}. We demonstrate that these metrics can quantify the proportion of variability of the response explained by the predictions, in a similar manner as the predictive $R^2$ for continuous response variables. After establishing theoretical connections between the $\mathrm{RGX}_p$ family and other prominent metrics in AI, we conduct extensive experiments across diverse datasets and learning tasks to evaluate their empirical performance. ### [70] [Avoidance of non-strict saddle points by blow-up](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.23268)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用"爆破"技术，通过对目标函数进行非线性重缩放，使高阶几何结构变得可见。然后应用动力系统理论中的中心稳定流形定理来分析梯度流在非严格鞍点附近的行为。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种分析梯度流在非严格鞍点处行为的新方法，通过爆破技术结合中心稳定流形定理，解决了经典理论无法处理的退化情况，对机器学习和优化理论有重要意义。

Abstract: It is an old idea to use gradient flows or time-discretized variants thereof as methods for solving minimization problems. In some applications, for example in machine learning contexts, it is important to know that for generic initial data, gradient flow trajectories do not get stuck at saddle points. There are classical results concerned with the nondegenerate situation. But if the Hessian of the objective function has a nontrivial kernel at the critical point, then these results are inconclusive. In this paper, we show how relevant information can be extracted by ``blowing up'' the objective function around the non-strict saddle point, i.e., by a suitable nonlinear rescaling that makes the higher order geometry visible. Then the center-stable manifold theorem of dynamical system theory can be applied.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lusztig为有限箭图引入了量子群的几何实现并定义了它们的典范基。Sala和Schiffmann引入了线箭图的Ringel-Hall代数，并将其实现为A型有限箭图Ringel-Hall代数的直接极限。本文旨在通过Lusztig的几何实现方法，结合Sala和Schiffmann的近似方法，为A型连续箭图的Ringel-Hall代数提供几何实现。

Method: 采用Sala和Schiffmann提出的近似方法，利用Lusztig为有限箭图量子群建立的几何实现技术，将A型连续箭图的Ringel-Hall代数通过有限箭图的近似来构造几何实现。

Result: 成功实现了A型连续箭图Ringel-Hall代数的几何构造，将Lusztig的几何实现方法推广到连续箭图情形。

Conclusion: 本文通过结合Lusztig的几何实现和Sala-Schiffmann的近似方法，为A型连续箭图的Ringel-Hall代数建立了系统的几何实现框架，扩展了几何表示论的研究范围。

Abstract: Lusztig introduced the geometric realizations of quantum groups associated to finite quivers and defined their canonical bases. Sala and Schiffmann introduced the Ringel-Hall algebra of line and realized it as the direct limit of Ringel-Hall algebras of finite quivers of type $A$. In this paper, we shall give geometric realizations of Ringel-Hall algebras of continuous quivers of type $A$ via the geometric realizations of Lusztig by using the method of approximation given by Sala and Schiffmann.

</details>

### [74] [Lie groupoids, the Satake compactification and the tempered dual, II: The Harish-Chandra principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22635)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用Satake紧化、本系列第一篇论文中构造的相关群胚及其C*代数，从几何角度分析表示理论

Conclusion: 几何方法为理解实约化群的表示理论提供了新视角，将代数表示论与几何结构联系起来

Abstract: We give a geometric account of Harish-Chandra's principle that a tempered irreducible representation of a real reductive group is either square-integrable modulo center, or embeddable in a representation that is parabolically induced from such a representation. Our approach uses the Satake compactification, an associated groupoid that was constructed in the first paper of this series, and its $C^*$-algebra.

### [75] [Lie groupoids, the Satake compactification and the tempered dual, I: The Satake groupoid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.22637)
*Jacob Bradd,Nigel Higson,Robert Yuncken*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文从三个不同视角研究了与实约化群G相关的Satake紧化的群胚结构，并计划在后续论文中应用该群胚给出Harish-Chandra原理的新证明


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Satake紧化的群胚结构，为理解实约化群的表示理论提供新的几何视角，特别是为Harish-Chandra原理（所有缓增不可约表示可通过离散序列表示的抛物诱导构造）提供新证明

Method: 1. 作为拓扑群胚定义Satake群胚（Omar Mohsen一般构造的特例）；2. 从李理论角度描述Satake群胚（借鉴Toshio Oshima的工作）；3. 将Satake群胚与Satake紧化的纯几何b-群胚等同，利用紧化作为带角光滑流形的结构

Result: 建立了Satake紧化的三种等价群胚描述：拓扑群胚构造、李理论描述、几何b-群胚等同，为后续表示理论研究提供了统一的群胚框架

Conclusion: Satake紧化具有丰富的群胚结构，该结构可从拓扑、李理论和几何三个不同视角理解，为后续应用（特别是Harish-Chandra原理的新证明）奠定了理论基础

Abstract: The (maximal) Satake compactification associated to a real reductive group $G$ is the closure of the symmetric space of all maximal compact subgroups of $G$ within the compact space of all closed subgroups of $G$. We shall present three different views of a groupoid that may be associated to the Satake compactification. To begin, we shall define our Satake groupoid, as we shall call it, as a topological groupoid, and as a special case of a general construction of Omar Mohsen. Then we shall give a Lie-theoretic account of the Satake groupoid, borrowing from work of Toshio Oshima. Finally we shall identify the Satake groupoid with the purely geometric $b$-groupoid of the Satake compactification, using the structure of the compactification as a smooth manifold with corners. In a subsequent paper we shall use the Satake groupoid to present a new proof of Harish-Chandra's principle, that all the tempered irreducible representations of $G$ may be constructed from discrete series representations using parabolic induction.

</details>

### [76] [The impact of magnetic fields during tidal disruption events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.21818)
*Simona Pacuraru,Clément Bonnerot,Martin E. Pessah*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过磁流体动力学模拟和半解析模型，分析了恒星潮汐瓦解事件中磁场对碎片流演化的影响，发现强磁场会导致碎片流快速增厚，可能影响后续的射电辐射和气体动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究恒星潮汐瓦解事件中磁场在碎片流演化过程中的动态重要性，特别是强磁场如何影响碎片流的厚度和后续演化。

Method: 使用磁流体动力学模拟和半解析模型，研究主序星被超大质量黑洞瓦解的过程，分析磁场强度对碎片流厚度的影响。

Result: 当恒星磁场强度超过约10^4 G时，磁压变得重要，导致碎片流厚度快速增加，宽度随黑洞距离呈H ∝ R^{5/4}关系增长。

Conclusion: 磁场在潮汐瓦解事件中具有重要动力学作用，为后续研究提供了考虑磁场的物理初始条件，有助于理解磁场在角动量输运和可观测特征中的作用。

Abstract: During a tidal disruption event (TDE) the stream debris inherits the magnetic field of the star. As the stream stretches, the magnetic field evolves and can eventually become dynamically important. We study this effect by means of magnetohydrodynamic simulations and a semi-analytic model of the disruption of a main-sequence star by a supermassive black hole. For stellar magnetic fields stronger than $\sim 10^4\,\rm{G}$, magnetic pressure becomes important in a significant fraction of the mass of the stream, leading to a fast increase in its thickness, an effect that may impact its subsequent evolution. We find that this dynamical effect is associated with a phase of transverse equilibrium between magnetic and tidal forces, which causes the stream width to increase with distance to the black hole as $H \propto R^{5/4}$. In the unbound tail, this fast expansion could enhance the radio emission produced by the interaction with the ambient medium, while in the returning stream, it may qualitatively affect the subsequent gas evolution, particularly the gas dynamics and radiative properties of shocks occurring after the stream's return to pericentre. By characterizing the magnetohydrodynamic properties of the stream from disruption to the first return to pericentre, this work provides physically motivated initial conditions for future studies of the later phases of TDEs, accounting for magnetic fields. This will ultimately shed light on the role of magnetic fields in enabling angular momentum transport in the ensuing accretion disk, thereby affecting observable signatures such as X-ray radiation and relativistic outflows.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究不同内部结构的恒星前身星在核心坍缩过程中产生的引力波信号差异，探索引力波探测能否提供恒星内部结构信息。

Result: 更紧凑的前身星产生更大振幅的引力波应变和更高的引力波能量释放，其g-/f-模式特征的演化斜率比不紧凑模型大26%。

Conclusion: 引力波探测在原则上可以提供关于恒星内部结构的信息，不同内部结构的前身星会产生可区分的引力波信号特征。

Abstract: We present the gravitational wave predictions from two-dimensional core collapse supernova (CCSN) simulations initiated from two nearly identical progenitors that have significantly different internal structures due to their late-stage stellar evolution. At the time of collapse, the 15.78 $M_{\odot}$ and 15.79 $M_{\odot}$ progenitors have compactness parameters $ξ_{2.5}$ of 0.136 and 0.206, respectively. We connect several features of the gravitational wave signal from each model to its previously explored explosion dynamics. In particular, the greater accretion onto the PNS of the more compact model is evident in broad-band frequency features with larger amplitude gravitational wave strains and greater gravitational wave energy release when compared to the less compact model. Additionally, the faster contraction rate of the more compact model is reflected in the $\sim$26% greater slope of the $g$-/$f$-mode feature (gfF) evolution of the gravitational wave signal. This work shows that in principle gravitational wave detection may provide information about interior stellar structure.
